### NOTE ###

The verification logs contains the following errors:

ERROR: test_ip_output (vmtests.test_network_vlan.GroovyTestNetworkVlan)
ERROR: test_ip_output (vmtests.test_network_ipv6_vlan.GroovyTestNetworkIPV6Vlan)
ERROR: test_ip_output (vmtests.test_network_ipv6.GroovyTestNetworkIPV6)

and its final status is therefore reported as FAILURE. The errors are
due to skip_by_date statements that passed their 'removeby' date, e.g.

RuntimeError: skip_by_date(test_ip_output.test_ip_output) LP: #1888726
    fixby=2020-10-15 removeby=2020-11-05: (REMOVE_WORKAROUND) Passed.

LP: #1888726 is now fixed and the skip_by_date removed in curtin master.
